<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развеваться.html>развева́ться</a> (11462)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">развева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеваться.html>развева́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvevátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеяться.html>разве́яться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flutter, to fly, to stream</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scatter, to disperse, to dissipate</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведённый.html>разведённый</a> (2506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***разведать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведать.html>разве́дать</a> (16942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разведать.html>разве́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvédatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разве́дывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find out <i>(about)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reconnoitre, to reconnoiter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prospect, to explore
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разведать.html>разве́дать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:район.html>райо́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нефть.html>нефть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvédatʹ</b> rajón na neftʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prospect a district for oil</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разведанный.html>разве́данные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нефть.html>не́фти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razvédannyje zapásy néfti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">explored/known oil reserves</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">развед-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razved-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведывательный.html>разве́дывательный</a> (8690)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разве́дывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvédyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разведывательный.html>разве́дывательный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvédyvatelʹnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reconnaissance, intelligence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разведывательный.html>разве́дывательный</a></b> полёт</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvédyvatelʹnyj</b> poljót</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>reconnaissance</b> flight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разведывательный.html>разве́дывательная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvédyvatelʹnaja</b> slúžba</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>intelligence</b> service</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:центральный.html>центра́льное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разведывательный.html>разве́дывательное</a> управле́ние‎</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Centrálʹnoje razvédyvatelʹnoje upravlénije‎</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Intelligence_Agency" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Central Intelligence Agency">Central Intelligence Agency</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***развезти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развезти.html>развезти́</a> (17576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развезти.html>развезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развозить.html>развози́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deliver, to transport (multiple people or things to their respective destinations)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развезти.html>развезло́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>razvezló</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he grew weak and limp (from); he became tipsy/obfuscated/muddled/woozy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make impassable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развезти.html>развезло́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dorógu <b>razvezló</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the road became impassable</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезти́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poveztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***развернуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a> (2799)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертывать.html>развёртывать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачивать.html>развора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to unroll, to unwind, to unfold, to unwrap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> kovjór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unroll a carpet</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> gazétu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unfold the paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пакет.html>паке́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> pakét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unwrap a parcel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>знамёна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> znamjóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spread out the banners</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to show, to display
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show/display/reveal one's strength</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> svoj talánt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show/display one's talent</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to start <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> svojó délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to start up a business of one's own</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put on a wide scale, to widen, to broaden, to expand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:торговля.html>торго́влю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> torgóvlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to expand trade</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широко</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">široko <b>razvernútʹ</b> rabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to place the work on a broad footing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́мму</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обучение.html>обуче́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvernútʹ</b> širókuju prográmmu obučénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put in place a large-scale training programme</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deploy, to extend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expand <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to turn, to swing about, to swing around, to slew <i>(about)</i>, to make a U-turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ло</a></b> поперёк <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>дороги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašínu <b>razvernúlo</b> poperjók dorogi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the car veered across the road</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***развернуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развернуться.html>разверну́ться</a> (3565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуться.html>разверну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертываться.html>развёртываться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разворачиваться.html>развора́чиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn around, to swing about / around; to make a U-turn (vehicle); to slew (about)</li>
<li>to be deployed (of troops)</li>
<li>to come unrolled / unfolded / unwrapped</li>
<li>to spread, to expand</li>
<li>to display oneself</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развернуть.html>разверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ol><li>-</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертывание.html>развёртывание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvjórtyvanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертывание.html>развёртывания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертывание.html>развёртывания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развертывание.html>развёртываний</a></b>)

***развесить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развесить.html>разве́сить</a> (11800)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развесить.html>разве́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvésitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развешивать.html>разве́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to weigh out</li>
<li>to hang <i>(in different places)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развесить.html>разве́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvésitʹ</b> úši</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to listen open-mouthed; to let oneself be duped/fooled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(boughs)</i> to spread, to stretch out</li></ol>

***развести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развести.html>развести́</a> (2506)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развести.html>развести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разводить.html>разводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take along, to bring; to conduct</li>
<li>to part, to move apart, to pull apart, to separate</li>
<li>to dilute, to mix</li>
<li>to dissolve</li>
<li>to start</li>
<li>to divorce</li>
<li>to mount, to relieve, to post (sentinels)</li>
<li>to rear, to breed (animals)</li>
<li>to plant, to cultivate, to grow (plants)</li>
<li>to make, to plant, to lay out (a park, garden, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cheat, to swindle</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разведение.html>разведе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvedénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развод.html>разво́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разводка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvodka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развестись.html>развести́сь</a> (7029)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развести.html>развести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развестись.html>развести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разводиться.html>разводи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be divorced, to divorce, to obtain a divorce <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развестись.html>развела́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:муж.html>му́жем</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>razvelásʹ</b> s múžem.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>divorced</b> her husband.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to grow in number, to breed</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развести.html>развести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разветвить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разветвить.html>разветви́ть</a> (25770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ветви́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vetvítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разветвить.html>разветви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvetvítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разветвля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cause to branch out, to cause to ramify</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to divide into separate industries</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разветвлённый.html>разветвлённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvetvljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разветвить.html>разветви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvetvítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разветвлённый.html>разветвлённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvetvljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>extensive, far-flung</li>
<li>ramified
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разветвлённый.html>разветвлённая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́ма</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvetvljónnaja</b> sistéma/setʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ramified system/network</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***развешивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развешивать.html>разве́шивать</a> (18671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развесить.html>разве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; in the meaning "to hang (something) out", also from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развешать.html>разве́шать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvéšatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развешивать.html>разве́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvéšivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развесить.html>разве́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to weigh out</li>
<li>to hang <i>(in different places)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развесить.html>разве́сить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razvésitʹ úši</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to listen open-mouthed; to let oneself be duped/fooled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(boughs)</i> to spread, to stretch out</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разве́ска</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvéska</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">развесно́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvesnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***развеять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развеять.html>разве́ять</a> (13504)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веять.html>ве́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеять.html>разве́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvéjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разве́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scatter, to disperse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развеять.html>разве́ял</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:облако.html>облака́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>razvéjal</b> oblaká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind <b>dispersed</b> the clouds</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dispel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:развеять.html>разве́ять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:миф.html>миф</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razvéjatʹ</b> mif</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>explode/discredit/shatter</b> the myth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cast away, to lay aside, to put out of mind</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wave <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. a flag</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">развева́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cause to flutter or blow about
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">развева́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веять.html>ве́ять</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">véjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прове́ять</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">provéjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веяние.html>ве́яние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">véjanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:развеяться.html>разве́яться</a> (21885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеять.html>разве́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvéjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеяться.html>разве́яться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razvéjatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разве́иваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scatter, to disperse, to dissipate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>ту́ман</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развеяться.html>разве́ялся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">túman <b>razvéjalsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the fog <b>dissipated</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to be dispelled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:развеяться.html>разве́ялся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó pečálʹ <b>razvéjalsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his sadness <b>was dispelled</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be distracted from one's cares, to have fun</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flutter, to blow about
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеваться.html>развева́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razvevátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развеять.html>разве́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razvéjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
